Attacks mode allow the player to loot gold, elixir and have a maximum timed length of 5 minutes.\r\nYou can also choose to play tower defend style to stop waves of attacking militias. \r\n\r\n\r\nBuildings\r\nThe game has 1 ’builders’ by default, but the player can install more builders (maximum 4) by buying them at an increasing number of gems. Builders are important for upgrading any building. If all builders are busy upgrading a building, one has to either wait (if the player wants to upgrade a different building) for them to be free or complete another building’s upgrade using gems. There are a number of buildings available to the player to defend their village, including cannons, heavy bow, archer towers. Players can also build walls, which can be upgraded as a player’s town hall level increases.\r\n\r\nResources\r\nTo earn and store gold and elixir, players must build gold mines and gold storages and elixir collectors and elixir storages, respectively. Resources is used to train new troops, new defend turrets and carry out building upgrades. \r\n\r\nTroops \r\nThe game has two kinds of building for building troops, barracks to train different types of soldiers, and Army Camp to house the soldiers. Different Town hall levels are required before you can train footman, archer, gryphon, knights, paladin, siege tank and Dragons.\r\n\r\n\r\nGems\r\nAside from the game’s resources (gold, elixir), the game also uses gems as a currency. Gems may be used primarily to finish the time that certain processes take, such as the remaining time of a building’s or a troop’s upgrade, or to instantly train an army. \r\n\r\nControl\r\nPC Desktop, use mouse to select, move the building, zoom camera view. Click on the ground to unselect.\r\nXBOX One, use the controller left joystick to move the cursor and select with A button. Select any ground on the map to de-select.\r\n\r\nGuild\r\nBuild a guild house to enable this function. Enter guild to chat with other players.\r\n\r\nTravel \r\nBuild a Air depot to enable travel.\r\nTravel to other players castle to visit or loot.\r\n\r\nAttack\r\nSelect troop types ( more then 1 unit) and place on map, the troop will move and attack automatically.\r\n\r\nXBOX One, use the X button to launch troop. A Button to select.\r\n\r\nSetting\r\nSwitch game sound effects ON or OFF.\r\nSwitch game background music ON or OFF.\r\n\r\nHELP\r\nProvides quick start instructions.\r\n\r\nXBOX LIVE Services\r\n-
